 jab stadium kii prashaasak se is bare main aaj tak ne baat kii to unhone kaha ki yah vibhaag kaa aantarik masalaa he
 He has been entrusted with this responsibility in the spare time of the coaches
 jisase unka behatar upyog kiya ja sake
 a coach told Aaj Tak on condition of anonymity of Manjushri's name in the stadium that these days, Coaches are going through a lot of mental torture
 jisaki vajah se wo apane koching ke kaam par sahi tareeke se dhyaan nahin de paa rahe hai
 Those coaches are facing the most problem
 jinaki duty hostal main lagaai gai he
 The hostel is frequented by players and teams day and night
 kamare kii safa safai se lekar bathrum main tauliye tak kii jimmedaari coach par daali gai he
 It is bound to raise a question, is this the job of a coach? Why Sai and the Sports Ministry are sitting close to their eyes kya bhartiya khel praadhikaran ke paas apane kochej ko kis tarah se istemaal main laayaa jaae
 They do not have a plan for this
 dronacharya kaise taiyaar karenge arjuna?jis desh main khilaadiyon or unke guruon ke saath aisa durvyavhaar ho rahaa ho
 How can any great expectation be placed there
 olympic or asian khelon ke dauraan mantri, adhikari badi-badi bate karte hai
 The headlines are made, no one accidentally retracts today in taking a medal and even taking a photo with the player, making big announcements
 maanon medal inhen kii badaulat aayaa ho
 But the state of sports in India and the thinking of the officials who run the games are not hidden from anyone
 yah uskaa ek or udhaaharan he
 Such stories not only reflect the apathy and thinking of the officials who run the game
 balki khel khilaadiyon or khel premiyon kaa dil bhi todatii hai
 One thing is clear, this kind of arrangement cannot improve the state of sports in the country
 sirf bade-bade elaan hi ho sakate hai
 Kevin Pietersen's stormy century saw the Delhi Daredevils recover from the odds, beating the Deccan Chargers by five wickets in the Indian Premier League match on Thursday and extending their wait for the first win
 petersan ne chah, 68 or 94 ran ke nijee score par mili jeevandaan kaa phayda uthaate hue 64 gend main nau chhakkon or chah chaukon kii madad se naabad 103 ran kii pari kheli jisase dilli kii team ne paanch gend shesh rahete paanch wicket par 162 ran banaakar match jeet liya
 Pietersen, the first Delhi batsman to score more than 50 runs in IPL five, scored 42 with Ross Taylor (13), 49 with Irfan Pathan (05) and 4 with Yogesh Nagar (23 not out, 15 balls, three fours)
 3 over main 48 ran kii atoot saajhedaari kii
 Earlier, the Chargers scored 157 for eight with the help of excellent innings by Parthiv Patel (45) and Shikhar Dhawan (44)
 dilli kii ore se nadeem ne 16 ran dekar teen jabaki morkal ne 23 ran dekar teen wicket chatkaakar chargers ko bada score banane se roka
 This is Delhi's fourth win in five matches and has topped the table with eight points while the Chargers' team is on the final spot after a fourth defeat in four matches
 dilli kii shuruuaat kharaab rahi or usne paanchaven over main 23 ran ke score tak hi donon salaami ballebaajon naman ojha (01) or captain virendra sahvaag (07) ke alaava mahela jayavardhane (06) kaa wicket ganvaa diya
 Jayawardene also caught a catch from fellow Christian Sri Lankan and Chargers captain Kumar Sangakkara at mid-off
 petersan or tailor ne wicket girane kaa kram roka
 Taylor hit a four off Pratap Singh on the first ball while Pietersen added 17 runs including a four and two sixes in his over, targeting leg-spinner Amit Mishra
 tailor christian ke over main tej ran lene ke prayaas main dhawan ke sateek nishane kaa shikaar banakar pavilion laute
 Duminy's 13th over of the innings was eventful
 petersan ne pehali gend ko long aaf main ek ran ke liye khelkar 42 gend par ardhashatak puraa kiya
 He then hit three consecutive sixes in the same over and reached the team's score of 100 runs
 dumini ne haalanki agali gend par is ballebaaj kaa kaich tapakaa diya
 Delhi needed 54 runs to win in the last seven overs and in such a situation, Pietersen made it easy for the team to hit Mishra for six but Pathan (05) caught Parthiv Patel behind the wicket in an attempt to pull Stan's ball
 Sitting
 petersan ne iske baad vir pratap singh or christian par chakke jade jisase team ko antim do over main jeet ke liye aath ran kii darkaar thi
 Pietersen scored a straight six over Ankit to complete the century and lead the team to victory
 england kaa yah ballebaaj ipel main shatak jadne vaala 18waan ballebaaj he
 After winning the toss, the Chargers, who came out to bat first, lost the wicket of Sangakkara (01) on the score of 10 runs in the third over
 dhawan or parthiv ne pari ko sambhala
 Both reached the team's score of 50 runs in six overs
 dhawan baayen haath ke spinner nadeem kii pehali hi gend ko reverse sweep karne ke prayaas main pagabaadha out ho gaye
 He hit five fours and a six in his 29-ball innings
 tippaniyan Parthiv hit Umesh for a six
 vah isi over kii antim gend par bhaagyashaalee rahe jab third main par agarkar ne unka kaich lapak liya lekin maidani ampiron ne tisare ampire se salaah ke baad qamar se upar gend ke liye ise nobal qaraar diya
 Parthiv, however, catches Jayawardene at deep square leg in an effort to hit a six in Nadeem's next over
 unhone 27 gend par paanch chauke or ek chakka jadaa
 After these two batsmen returned to the pavilion, the Delhi bowlers controlled the run pace
 dumini (04) nadeem kaa teesraa shikaar bane
 Christian (19) then caught trying to pull Umesh's ball while Morkel sent Abhishek Jhunjhunwala (04) and Dale Steyn (02) to the pavilion

 ye dekhbhaal unke swasthya par sabase adhik asar daalati he

 jisase pataa chalaa ki garib bacchon main motaape kaa khatra, samrudh bacchon kii tulana main doguna zyada tha

 9 percent were seen

 mughal badshaah shahjahan kii begum or tajmahal banane kii vajah baniin mumtaj mahal kaa intkaal saal 1631 main 17 june ko hua tha
 
 
 Know the special things about this Begum
 
 
 1
 Arjumand Banu Begum (mumtaz), coming from the family of Agra, married in 1612 at the age of 19 with Khurram (shah Jahan)
 2
 Shah Jahan handed over Mumtaz's personal property worth Rs 1 crore to his daughter Jahanara Begum
 3
 After this, Shah Jahan decided to build Taj Mahal in memory of Mumtaz, which took 22 years to build
 4
 She had 14 children, 19 of whom died at the age of 19, in Shaad
 5
 While giving birth to the 14th child (gauhra Begum), Mumtaz died in Burhanpur
 6
 Mumtaz's death pushed Shah Jahan into the darkness of sorrow
 saal bhar main unke bal safed ho gaye, qamar jhuk gai or chehre par jhurriyaan aa gayi
 7
 ulka pind iroj main do gaddhon ke namshahjahanor mumtaj ke naam par rakhe gaye
